 ) Scientists have achieved a major breakthrough and have discovered a new layer in the cornea of the eye, part of human anatomy, and have decided to name it after the Indian researcher who discovered it
 insaan kii aankh ke agle hisse ko cornia kaha jaataa he
 This discovery by researchers at the University of Nottingham in the UK will help doctors to get cornea grafting or give better results to patients who have undergone cornea transplantation
 cornia kii nai khoji gai is parat kaa naam 'dua' ja layer' rakhaa gaya he
 Professor Harminder Dua has discovered this
 isse pehle vaigyanikon ko cornia kii is parat ke bare main koi jaankaree nahin thi
 The cornea in the front of the eye is a clear protective lens through which light enters the eye
 pehle vaigyanikon kaa maananaa tha ki cornia kii aage se lekar peeche tak paanch paraten hoti hai, jinhen corneal apithelium , bomens layer, corneal stroma , disemets mambraine tathaa corneal endothelium kaha jaataa he
 The newly discovered layer lies between the corneal stroma and the desements
 haalanki yah keval 15 micrones motaai kii he lekin yah behad majboot he
 The thickness of the entire cornea is about 550 microns or 0
 5 mimi hoti he
 Professor Dua said that this is a major discovery which means that text books related to ophthalmology will need to be rewritten
 unhone bataaya, 'cornia ke uttakon kii gaharaai main is nayi or anokhi parat kii khoj ke baad , ab ham isaki dabaav sahane kii kshamta kaa istemaal kar marijon kii ankhon kaa aaparishan adhik surakshit or aasaan tareeke se karne kii sambhaavnaaon kaa pataa laga sakate hai
 'this research report has been published in the Journal of Ophthalmology

 How to donate for Shani Kripa on the Saturday of Saavan? - First worship Shiva by taking evening bath
 - iske baad pipal ke vriksh ke neeche sarson ke tel kaa deepak jalaaen
 - Chant Shani Mantra
 - iske baad shraddha bhav se kisi nirdhan yaa jaruratmand ko daan karen
 - Pray for the wish fulfillment in your heart
